the option\\n124:    * @param expiry the option expiry\\n125:    * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\\n126:    * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\\n127:    * @param strike the FX paymentDate,\\n141:       BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\\n142: \\n143:     ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \\\"Base notional must be positive\\\");\\n144:     ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \\\"FX strike must be positive\\\");\\n145: \\n146:     // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\\n148:     double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\\n149:     double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\\n150:     double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\\n151:     CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\\n152:     CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\\n153:     FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\\n162:         .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\\n163:         .build();\\n164:   }\\n165: \\n166:     // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n148:     double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n149:     double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n150:     double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n151:     CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n152:     CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n153:     FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n154:         FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n163:         .build();\n164:   }\n165: \n166:   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n167:   @ImmutableValidator\n168: option is a financial instrument that provides an option to exchange two currencies at a specified future time\\n39:  * only when barrier event occurs (knock-in option) or does not occur (knock-out option).\\n40:  * <p>\\n41:  * Depending on the barrier defined in {@link Barrier}, the options are classified into four types: up-and-in,\\n42:  * down-and-in, up-and-out and down-and-out.\\n43:  * <p>\\n44:  * For example, an up-and-out call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange with barrier of 1.5 is the option to\\n45:  * perform a foreign exchange on the expiry date, where USD 1.41 is paid to receive EUR 1.00, only when EUR/USD rate does\\n46:  * not exceed 1.5 during the barrier event observation period.\\n47:  * <p>\\n48:  * In case of the occurrence (non-occurrence for knock-in options) of the barrier event, the option becomes worthless,\\n49:  * or alternatively, a rebate is made.\\n50:  */\\n51: @BeanDefinition\\n52: public final class FxSingleBarrierOption\\n53:     implements stored in this field must be represented based on the direction of the currency pair in the\\n64:    * underlying FX transaction.\\n65:    * <p>\\n66:    * For example, if the underlying option is an option on EUR/GBP, the barrier should be a certain level of EUR/GBP rate.\\n67:    */\\n68:   @PropertyDefinition(validate = \\\"notNull\\\")\\n69:   private final Barrier barrier;\\n70:   /**\\n71:    * For a 'out' option, the amount is paid when the barrier is reached;\\n72:    * for a 'in' option, the amount is paid at expiry if the barrier is not reached.\\n73:    * <p>\\n74:    * This is the notional amount represented in one of the currency pair.\\n75:    * The amount should be positive.\\n76:    */\\n77:   @PropertyDefinition(get = \\\"optional\\\")\\n78:   private final CurrencyAmount rebate;\\n79: \\n80:   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n81:   /**\\n82:    * Obtains FX single barrier option with rebate.\\n83:    *\\n84:    * @param FxSingleBarrierOption of(FxVanillaOption underlyingOption, Barrier barrier, CurrencyAmount rebate) {\\n90:     return new FxSingleBarrierOption(underlyingOption, barrier, rebate);\\n91:   }\\n92:
